For each square foot of land, the heavy-duty yard machine requires 2 seconds while the gas lawn mower takes 5 seconds. Per square foot, the heavy-duty yard machine produces 12 units of pollution and requires 3 units of fuel. Conversely, the gas lawn mower generates 10 units of pollution for each square foot and requires 2 units of fuel. There are 450 units of fuel available and the landscaper can produce no more than 2000 units of pollution. For how many square feet should each machine be used to minimize the time required to cut this customers backyard?
N/A
```python

from cpmpy import Model, intvar

# Decision Variables
YardMachine = intvar(0, 2500)  # Square feet of grass cut using the heavy-duty yard machine
LawnMower = intvar(0, 2500)  # Square feet of grass cut using the gas lawn mower

# Constraints
m = Model()

# Total square feet of grass land should not exceed 2500:
m += YardMachine + LawnMower <= 2500

# Fuel constraint: 3 units of fuel per square foot for the yard machine, 2 units of fuel per square foot for the lawn mower, maximum 450 units available
m += 3 * YardMachine + 2 * LawnMower <= 450

# Pollution constraint: 12 units of pollution per square foot for the yard machine, 10 units of pollution per square foot for the lawn mower, maximum 2000 units allowed
m += 12 * YardMachine + 10 * LawnMower <= 2000

# Objective
# Minimize the total time required to cut the grass (2 seconds per square foot for the yard machine, 5 seconds per square foot for the lawn mower)
m.minimize(2 * YardMachine + 5 * LawnMower)

```
True

A park is designing their trails and can either create a wide trail or a narrow trail. A wide trail can take 50 visitors every day while the narrow trail expects 20 visitors every day. The wide trail will introduce 6 units of garbage and the narrow trail will introduce 3 units of garbage. There can be at most 3 wide trails and the park hopes to have at most 225 visitors every day. How many of each type of trail should the park construct to minimize the total amount of garbage produced.
N/A
```python

from cpmpy import Model, intvar

# Decision Variables
WideTrails = intvar(0, 3)  # Number of wide trails
NarrowTrails = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of narrow trails

# Constraints
m = Model()

# Total number of visitors should be at most 225 per day:
m += 50 * WideTrails + 20 * NarrowTrails <= 225
# Total amount of garbage produced should be minimized:
m.minimize(6 * WideTrails + 3 * NarrowTrails)

```
True
True
Wrong: 1, Total: 2, Is objective correct: True

A brewery can ferment their product into either wine or kombucha. Each unit of wine requires 3 units of fruit and 8 units of water. Each unit of kombucha requires 5 units of fruit and 7 units of tea. The company has available 7000 units of water and 9000 units of tea. Wine sells for more, therefore the number of wine must be larger than the number of kombucha. Additionally, at least 20% of their products made must be kombucha. How many of each should the brewery make to minimize the total units of fruit required?
N/A
```python

from cpmpy import Model, intvar

# Decision Variables
Wine = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of units of wine
Kombucha = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of units of kombucha

# Constraints
m = Model()

# Fruit and water constraints for wine and kombucha:
m += 3 * Wine + 5 * Kombucha <= 9000  # Fruit constraint
m += 8 * Wine + 7 * Kombucha <= 7000  # Water constraint

# At least 20% of the products must be kombucha:
m += Kombucha >= 0.2 * (Wine + Kombucha)

# Objective
# Minimize total units of fruit required:
m.minimize(3 * Wine + 5 * Kombucha)

```
False
False
Wrong: 3, Total: 4, Is objective correct: True

A hospital can transport their patients either using a type II ambulance or hospital van. The hospital needs to transport 320 patients every day. A type II ambulance is mounted on a truck-style chassis and can move 20 patients every shift and costs the hospital (including gas and salary) $820. A hospital van can move 15 patients and costs the hospital $550 every shift. The hospital can have at most 60% of shifts be hospital vans due to union limitations of the type II ambulance drivers. How many of shift using each type of vehicle should be scheduled to minimize the total cost to the hospital?
N/A
```python

from cpmpy import Model, intvar

# Decision Variables
AmbulanceShifts = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of shifts using type II ambulance
VanShifts = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of shifts using hospital van

# Constraints
m = Model()

# Total number of patients to transport is 320 every day:
m += 20 * AmbulanceShifts + 15 * VanShifts == 320

# Cost constraint: minimize total cost
# (Type II ambulance costs $820 per shift, hospital van costs $550 per shift)
m.minimize(820 * AmbulanceShifts + 550 * VanShifts)

# Union limitation: at most 60% of shifts can be hospital vans
m += VanShifts <= 0.6 * (AmbulanceShifts + VanShifts)

```
False
False
Wrong: 1, Total: 2, Is objective correct: True

An incandescent bulb manufacturing company uses either an argon gas approach or halogen gas approach to fill their light bulbs. The argon gas approach uses 10 units of gas and 12 units of glass to make 2 light bulbs. The halogen gas approach uses 12 units of gas and 8 units of glass to make 3 light bulbs. Additionally, the argon gas approach generates 3 units of heat while the halogen gas approach creates 4 units of heat. The manufacturing company has available 150 units of gas and 120 units of glass. If at most 28 units of heat can be generated during the manufacturing process, how many of each method should be used to maximize the number of light bulbs produced?
N/A
```python

from cpmpy import Model, intvar

# Decision Variables
ArgonApproach = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of light bulbs made using argon gas approach
HalogenApproach = intvar(0, 999999999)  # Number of light bulbs made using halogen gas approach

# Constraints
m = Model()

# Gas usage constraints (10 units for 2 bulbs with argon, 12 units for 3 bulbs with halogen, max 150 units available):
m += 5 * ArgonApproach + 4 * HalogenApproach <= 150
# Glass usage constraints (12 units for 2 bulbs with argon, 8 units for 3 bulbs with halogen, max 120 units available):
m += 6 * ArgonApproach + 8 * HalogenApproach <= 120
# Heat generation constraints (3 units for argon, 4 units for halogen, max 28 units allowed):
m += 3 * ArgonApproach + 4 * HalogenApproach <= 28

# Objective
# Maximize the number of light bulbs produced (2 bulbs for argon, 3 bulbs for halogen):
m.maximize(2 * ArgonApproach + 3 * HalogenApproach)

```
True
True
Wrong: 2, Total: 3, Is objective correct: True
